Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Link with onclick but no href is not keyboard accessible

<a class="nav-link studenter-link" onclick="_sz.push(['event', 'Hovedmeny', 'Klikk på lenke', 'For studenter']);" onkeydown="handleEnter(event)" tabindex="0">For studenter <i class="fas fa-chevron-rig
Add href attribute or use a button element
